      function getQueryStrings() { 
        var assoc  = {};
        var decode = function (s) { return decodeURIComponent(s.replace(/\+/g, " ")); };
        var queryString = location.search.substring(1); 
        var keyValues = queryString.split('&');

      for(var i in keyValues) {
      var key = keyValues[i].split('=');
      if (key.length > 1) {
      assoc[decode(key[0])] = decode(key[1]);
      }
      }

      return assoc;
      }
      if(window.location.href.indexOf("culture") != -1) {
      var qs = getQueryStrings();
      var myCulture = qs["culture"];

      if(myCulture.toUpperCase() == "TH-TH") {
      var urlRedirect=window.location.href.replace(myCulture,"en-TT");
      window.location = urlRedirect
      }
      }

      if ($('#imagePath') != null && $('#imagePath').length > 0 && $('#imagePath').val() != "")
      {
      SKYSALES.PreLoadImage();
      SKYSALES.DisplayImageLoadingBar();
      }
      else
      {
      SKYSALES.DisplayLoadingBar();
      }

      SKYSALES.checkSSOStatus();

      SKYSALES.datepicker = {};
      SKYSALES.datepicker.datePickerFormat = '';
      SKYSALES.datepicker.datePickerDelimiter = '';

      if (SKYSALES.datepicker.datePickerFormat.length !== 3)
      {
      SKYSALES.datepicker.datePickerFormat = 'mdy';
      SKYSALES.datepicker.datePickerDelimiter = '/';
      }
      SKYSALES.datepicker.closeText = 'Close';

      // string.padLeft function
      String.prototype.padLeft = function(l,c) {return Array(l-this.length+1).join(c||" ")+this}
      
      $( document ).ready(function() {
      marketDate = $('[class*="dayHeaderTodayImage"] [class*="todayDate"]');
      if (marketDate.length > 1)
      {
      //get and assign departure date to textbox
      departDate = $('[class*="dayHeaderTodayImage"] [class*="todayDate"]')[0].innerHTML.split('/');
      if (departDate.length != 3) return false;
      $('[id$=date_picker_display_id_1]').val(departDate[1].padLeft(2,'0') + '/' + departDate[0].padLeft(2,'0') + '/' + departDate[2]);
      $('[id$=date_picker_display_id_1]').trigger('change');
      
      //get and assign return date to textbox
      returnDate = $('[class*="dayHeaderTodayImage"] [class*="todayDate"]')[1].innerHTML.split('/');
      if (returnDate.length != 3) return false;
      $('[id$=date_picker_display_id_2]').val(returnDate[1].padLeft(2,'0') + '/' + returnDate[0].padLeft(2,'0') + '/' + returnDate[2]);
      $('[id$=date_picker_display_id_2]').trigger('change');
      }
      else if (marketDate.length == 1)
      {
      //get and assign departure date to textbox
      departDate = $('[class*="dayHeaderTodayImage"] [class*="todayDate"]')[0].innerHTML.split('/');
      if (departDate.length != 3) return false;
      $('[id$=date_picker_display_id_1]').val(departDate[1].padLeft(2,'0') + '/' + departDate[0].padLeft(2,'0') + '/' + departDate[2]);
      $('[id$=date_picker_display_id_1]').trigger('change');
      }
      });

      function makeFare(code, name, textArray)
      {
        this.code = code;
        this.name = name;
        this.text = new Array();
        this.text = textArray;
      }

      function displayCityInfo(market, fltType, station, arriveTime, deptTime, layoverTime, dropTime)
      {
        var direction = "";
        var message	= "";

        if (market == 1)
        {
          direction	= "outbound";
        }
        else if (market == 2)
        {
          direction	= "return";
        }

        if (fltType == "Leave")
        {
          message	= message + "This " + direction + " flight will begin \n";
          message = message + "in " + station + ".\n\n";
          message = message + "Departure time is at " + deptTime + ".";
        }
        else if (fltType == "Thru")
        {
          message	= message + "This " + direction + " flight will stop for a layover \n";
          message	= message + "in " + station + ".\n\n";
          message = message + "Estimated arrival time is " + dropTime + ".\n";
          message = message + "Departure time is at " + deptTime + ".\n";
          message = message + "Total layover time is " + layoverTime + ".\n\n";
          message = message + "There will be a brief stop in \n this city, but the trip will \n continue on the same plane" + ".";
        }
        else if (fltType == "Connect")
        {
          message	= message + "This " + direction + " flight will stop for a connection \n";
          message = message + "in " + station + ".\n\n";
          message = message + "Estimated arrival time is " + dropTime + ".\n";
          message = message + "Departure time is at " + deptTime + ".\n";
          message = message + "Total layover time is " + layoverTime + ".\n\n";
          message = message + "A Connection is scheduled to occur here. \nThis means that passengers will need to \nexit one plane and board another upon \narrival at this airport.  No need worry; our \nflights are arranged to give passengers \nample time to travel from one gate to \nanother." + "";
        }
        else if (fltType == "Arrive")
        {
          message	= message + "This " + direction + " flight will terminate \n";
          message = message + "in " + station + ".\n\n";
          message = message + "Estimated arrival time is " + arriveTime + ".";
			}
			alert (message)
			}
			
			
			function ferryTransferDisplayMouseover(caller,flightNO){
			var fareDescTop = parseInt($('#operatedBy_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).offset().top - 420) + "px";
			var fareDescLeft = parseInt($('#operatedBy_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).offset().left - 130) + "px";
      
      $('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).css({
      "top": fareDescTop,
      "left": fareDescLeft
      });
      $('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).show();
      }

      function ferryTransferDisplayMouseout(caller,flightNO){
      if (caller) {
      if ($('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).length > 0) {
      $('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).hide();
      }
      }
      }

      function ferryTransferDisplayMouseover2(caller,flightNO){
      var fareDescTop = parseInt($('#operatedBy_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).offset().top - 840) + "px";
			var fareDescLeft = parseInt($('#operatedBy_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).offset().left - 130) + "px";
      
      $('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).css({
      "top": fareDescTop,
      "left": fareDescLeft
      });
      $('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).show();
      }

      function ferryTransferDisplayMouseout2(caller,flightNO){
      if (caller) {
      if ($('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).length > 0) {
      $('#ferryTransferPromoter_' + caller+'_'+flightNO).hide();
      }
      }
      }
      
			
      function displayFlightInfo(airline, flightNum, departureStation, arrivalStation, equipment, airTimeHour, airTimeMinutes)
      {
        var message	= "Flight Details" + "\n\n"
        message = message + "This is " + airline + ", "
        message = message + "Flight " + flightNum + ", \n"
        message = message + "flying from " + departureStation + "\n"
        message = message + "to " + arrivalStation + ".\n\n"
        message = message + "The plane type is " + equipment + ".\n"
        message = message + "Estimated flight time is " + airTimeHour + " Hrs"
        message = message + " " + airTimeMinutes + " Mins."
      alert (message)
      }

      function setTabIndex(marketIndex, index, selectable)
      {
      if(selectable != 'FALSE')
      {
      if(marketIndex == 1) {
      $('input[id*=HiddenFieldTabIndex1]').val(index);
      }
      else {
      $('input[id*=HiddenFieldTabIndex2]').val(index);
      }
      postBack();
      }
      else
      {
      alert("Sorry, flights for this date are no longer available for booking.");
        }
        }


        function postBack()
        {
        __doPostBack('ControlGroupSelectView$AvailabilityInputSelectView$LinkButtonDateTab','');
      }

      var str = '';
      if ($('#AvSearch2').length>0 && $('#marketDate_2').length>0)
      {
      str = $('#marketDate_2').html();
      $('#AvSearch2').html(str);
      $('#marketDate_2').html('');
      $('#RoundTripContainer').hide('');
      }
      if ($('#AvSearch1').length>0 && $('#flightSearch1').length>0)
      {
      str = $('#flightSearch1').html();
      $('#AvSearch1').html(str);
      $('#flightSearch1').html('');
      }
      if ($('#AvSearch1').length>0 && $('#flightSearchBtn').length>0)
      {
      cur = $('#currencyDropDown').html();
      str = $('#flightSearchBtn').html();
      $('#AvSearch1').append(str);
      $('#marketDate_1').append(cur);
      $('#currencyDropDown').html('');
      }
      if ($('#AvSearch2').length>0 && $('#flightSearchBtn').length>0)
      {
      str = $('#flightSearchBtn').html();
      $('#AvSearch2').append(str);
      btn_id = $("#AvSearch2 input[@type='submit']").attr('id');
      $("#AvSearch2 input[@type='submit']").attr('id',btn_id+'2');
      }
      if ($('#flightSearchBtn').length>0)
      {
      $('#flightSearchBtn').html('');
      }
      if ($('#AvSearch1').length>0)
      {
      if ($('#AvSearch1').html().length < 5)
      {
      $('#AvSearch1').hide();
      $('#marketHeader1').show();
      }
      }
      if ($('#AvSearch2').length>0)
      {
      if ($('#AvSearch2').html().length < 5)
      {
      $('#AvSearch2').hide();
      }
      }

      toExpandDiv.click(function(){
        var parent = toExpandDiv.parent('.acccLinerTextFlexi');

        parent.addClass('expandText');

      function showSSRs(e, checkbox, bool)
      {

      if(!document.getElementById || !document.createTextNode)
      {
      return true;
      }

      var ds = document['SkySales'];
      var divSSRs	= document.getElementById('DivSSRs');

      if (bool)
      {
      // check the box, just in case
      ds['ControlGroupSelectView_SpecialNeedsInputSelectView_RadioButtonSSR'].selected = true;

          		// unhide the SSR list
          		divSSRs.style.display = "block";
      //document.getElementById('ssrRadiobutton').className = "ssrCheckboxSelected";
          	}
      else
      {
      // uncheck the box, just in case
      ds['ControlGroupSelectView_SpecialNeedsInputSelectView_RadioButtonSSR'].selected = false;
      // hide the SSR list
      divSSRs.style.display = "none";
      //document.getElementById('ssrRadiobutton').className = "ssrCheckbox";

          
          		// Also call document['SkySales'].submit(), so that we show all flights/call availability again
          		// but only when this function is not called by onLoad and there are ssr requests
          		// function SsrRequestsExists - existing function output by the control
          		if (e && e.type != 'onload' && e.type != null && SsrRequestsExists())
        			{
          			document['SkySales'].submit();
          		}

      }
      }
      function checkInt(textBox)
      {
      if (isNaN(parseInt(textBox.value)) || parseInt(textBox.value) < 0)
      {
      alert("\nHow many passengers need this service?  \n(Please enter a value of zero or higher.)");
      textBox.value = 0;
      textBox.select();
      }
      }

      var __doPostBack = function (eventTarget, eventArgument)
      {
      //added by Linson at 2012-01-09 begin
      SKYSALES.ReDisplayLoadingBar();
      //added by Linson at 2012-01-09 end
      var clearAllValidity = null;
      var eventTargetElement = window.document.getElementById('eventTarget');
      var eventArgumentElement = window.document.getElementById('eventArgument');
      var viewStateElement = window.document.getElementById('viewState');
      if (!theForm.onsubmit || (theForm.onsubmit() != false))
      {
      eventTargetElement.value = eventTarget || eventTargetElement.value;
      eventTargetElement.name = '__EVENTTARGET';
      if (eventArgument !== null)
      {
      eventArgumentElement.value = eventArgument;
      }
      eventArgumentElement.name = '__EVENTARGUMENT';
      viewStateElement.name = '__VIEWSTATE';
      if (theForm.checkValidity)
      {
      clearAllValidity = function ()
      {
      $(this).removeAttr("required");
      };
      SKYSALES.common.getAllInputObjects().each(clearAllValidity);
      }
      theForm.submit();
      }
      };
